It’s also possible to have GPS position continues.\r\nThere is also a search function to find places and locations on the map or from your loaded pois.\r\nIt is fully customizable for startup and home position and zoom levels. \r\nYou can use POI Viewer offline with maps and local copy of your files (after download of maps).\r\nPoiViewer10 can read GPS exchange format .gpx (Waypoints, Routes and Tracks), Garmin, .fit and .tcx files, Google Maps .kml and .kmz (Placemarks, Lines and Polygons), text files .csv and Tomtom .ov2 files.\r\nSupport png and bmp Icon file to poi file, and support for embedded Icons for kml and kmz files.\r\nIt's possible to open driving- and walking instructions and a point on the Windows mapping program. \r\nYou can record of your movements in a track on the map. If you have the PRO upgrade it’s possible to save it to a GPS exchange file (.gpx in track format) in the free version only the first 25 Track points will be saved. Auto save to _LastCreatedTrack.gpx in the open file list.\r\nNow it’s possible to measure distance on map by clicking on the map two or more times. In the free version only measure thru a straight line and in pro also via roads.\r\nSupport for Feedback app (require Windows 10 version 10.0.14271 or later)\r\nSupporting Windows INK, you can write with pen, mouse and touch on the map\r\nNow translated to more languages, PoiViwer10 will automatic select your language from French, German, Swedish, Spanish or Portuguese. previous loaded file\r\n- delete poi from map\r\n- edit poi name and description\r\n- move poi on map\r\n- save pois on map to new file in Garmin gpx, Tomtom ov2 and Google Maps kml format\r\n- split pois on map to several files (split on name, position north-south or west-east)\r\n- create your own poi file and save it to disk\r\n- send current loaded pois by email\r\n- every change is saved to
